{
  "file_path": "<AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>ns/mcp-server-semantic-analysis/src/workflow-runner.ts",
  "content": "#!/usr/bin/env node\n/**\n * Standalone workflow runner - runs in a separate process from MCP server\n * This allows workflows to survive MCP disconnections\n *\n * Usage: node workflow-runner.js <config-file-path>\n *\n * Config file is JSON with:\n * - workflowId: string\n * - workflowName: string\n * - repositoryPath: string\n * - parameters: object\n * - progressFile: string (where to write progress updates)\n */\n\nimport * as fs from 'fs';\nimport * as path from 'path';\nimport { CoordinatorAgent } from './agents/coordinator.js';\nimport { log } from './logging.js';\n\ninterface WorkflowConfig {\n  workflowId: string;\n  workflowName: string;\n  repositoryPath: string;\n  parameters: Record<string, any>;\n  progressFile: string;\n  pidFile: string;\n}\n\ninterface ProgressUpdate {\n  workflowId: string;\n  status: 'starting' | 'running' | 'completed' | 'failed';\n  currentStep?: string;\n  stepsCompleted?: number;\n  totalSteps?: number;\n  batchProgress?: {\n    currentBatch: number;\n    totalBatches: number;\n  };\n  message?: string;\n  error?: string;\n  startTime: string;\n  lastUpdate: string;\n  elapsedSeconds: number;\n  pid: number;\n}\n\nfunction writeProgress(progressFile: string, update: ProgressUpdate): void {\n  try {\n    fs.writeFileSync(progressFile, JSON.stringify(update, null, 2));\n  } catch (e) {\n    console.error('Failed to write progress:', e);\n  }\n}\n\nasync function main(): Promise<void> {\n  const configPath = process.argv[2];\n\n  if (!configPath) {\n    console.error('Usage: workflow-runner <config-file-path>');\n    process.exit(1);\n  }\n\n  let config: WorkflowConfig;\n\n  try {\n    const configContent = fs.readFileSync(configPath, 'utf-8');\n    config = JSON.parse(configContent);\n  } catch (e) {\n    console.error('Failed to read config file:', e);\n    process.exit(1);\n  }\n\n  const { workflowId, workflowName, repositoryPath, parameters, progressFile, pidFile } = config;\n\n  // Write PID file so parent can track us\n  fs.writeFileSync(pidFile, String(process.pid));\n\n  const startTime = new Date();\n\n  log(`[WorkflowRunner] Starting workflow: ${workflowName} (${workflowId})`, 'info', {\n    pid: process.pid,\n    repositoryPath,\n    parameters\n  });\n\n  // Initial progress update\n  writeProgress(progressFile, {\n    workflowId,\n    status: 'starting',\n    message: 'Initializing workflow runner...',\n    startTime: startTime.toISOString(),\n    lastUpdate: new Date().toISOString(),\n    elapsedSeconds: 0,\n    pid: process.pid\n  });\n\n  const coordinator = new CoordinatorAgent(repositoryPath);\n\n  try {\n    // Map workflow names\n    const workflowMapping: Record<string, { target: string; defaults: Record<string, any> }> = {\n      'complete-analysis': {\n        target: 'batch-analysis',\n        defaults: { fullAnalysis: true, resumeFromCheckpoint: false }\n      },\n      'incremental-analysis': {\n        target: 'batch-analysis',\n        defaults: { fullAnalysis: false, resumeFromCheckpoint: true }\n      },\n      'batch-analysis': { target: 'batch-analysis', defaults: {} }\n    };\n\n    const mapping = workflowMapping[workflowName];\n    const resolvedWorkflowName = mapping?.target || workflowName;\n    const resolvedParameters = mapping ? { ...mapping.defaults, ...parameters } : parameters;\n\n    // Get workflow info\n    const workflows = coordinator.getWorkflows();\n    const workflow = workflows.find(w => w.name === resolvedWorkflowName);\n    const isBatchWorkflow = workflow?.type === 'iterative' || resolvedWorkflowName === 'batch-analysis';\n\n    // Update progress to running\n    writeProgress(progressFile, {\n      workflowId,\n      status: 'running',\n      message: `Executing ${resolvedWorkflowName}...`,\n      startTime: startTime.toISOString(),\n      lastUpdate: new Date().toISOString(),\n      elapsedSeconds: Math.round((Date.now() - startTime.getTime()) / 1000),\n      pid: process.pid\n    });\n\n    // Execute the workflow\n    log(`[WorkflowRunner] Executing ${resolvedWorkflowName} (batch: ${isBatchWorkflow})`, 'info');\n\n    const execution = isBatchWorkflow\n      ? await coordinator.executeBatchWorkflow(resolvedWorkflowName, resolvedParameters)\n      : await coordinator.executeWorkflow(resolvedWorkflowName, resolvedParameters);\n\n    // Final success update\n    writeProgress(progressFile, {\n      workflowId,\n      status: execution.status === 'completed' ? 'completed' : 'failed',\n      currentStep: execution.currentStep,\n      stepsCompleted: execution.currentStep,\n      totalSteps: execution.totalSteps,\n      message: `Workflow ${execution.status}`,\n      startTime: startTime.toISOString(),\n      lastUpdate: new Date().toISOString(),\n      elapsedSeconds: Math.round((Date.now() - startTime.getTime()) / 1000),\n      pid: process.pid\n    });\n\n    log(`[WorkflowRunner] Workflow completed: ${execution.status}`, 'info', {\n      duration: `${Math.round((Date.now() - startTime.getTime()) / 1000)}s`,\n      steps: `${execution.currentStep}/${execution.totalSteps}`\n    });\n\n  } catch (error) {\n    const errorMessage = error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error);\n\n    writeProgress(progressFile, {\n      workflowId,\n      status: 'failed',\n      error: errorMessage,\n      message: `Workflow failed: ${errorMessage}`,\n      startTime: startTime.toISOString(),\n      lastUpdate: new Date().toISOString(),\n      elapsedSeconds: Math.round((Date.now() - startTime.getTime()) / 1000),\n      pid: process.pid\n    });\n\n    log(`[WorkflowRunner] Workflow failed: ${errorMessage}`, 'error', error);\n    process.exit(1);\n\n  } finally {\n    try {\n      await coordinator.shutdown();\n    } catch (e) {\n      log('[WorkflowRunner] Error during shutdown', 'error', e);\n    }\n\n    // Clean up PID file\n    try {\n      fs.unlinkSync(pidFile);\n    } catch (e) {\n      // Ignore\n    }\n\n    // Clean up config file\n    try {\n      fs.unlinkSync(configPath);\n    } catch (e) {\n      // Ignore\n    }\n  }\n}\n\n// Run main\nmain().catch(e => {\n  console.error('Fatal error in workflow runner:', e);\n  process.exit(1);\n});\n"
}

'‚úÖ' :\n                            runnerProgress.status === 'failed' ? '‚ùå' :\n                            runnerProgress.status === 'running' ? 'üîÑ' : '‚è∏Ô∏è';\n\n        let statusText = `# Workflow Status (Process-Isolated)\\n\\n`;\n        statusText += `**Workflow ID:** \\`${runnerProgress.workflowId}\\`\\n`;\n        statusText += `**Status:** ${statusEmoji} ${runnerProgress.status || 'unknown'}\\n`;\n        statusText += `**PID:** ${runnerProgress.pid || 'N/A'}\\n`;\n        statusText += `**Elapsed:** ${runnerProgress.elapsedSeconds || 0}s\\n`;\n        statusText += `**Started:** ${runnerProgress.startTime || 'N/A'}\\n`;\n        statusText += `**Last Update:** ${runnerProgress.lastUpdate || 'N/A'}\\n`;\n\n        if (runnerProgress.message) {\n          statusText += `**Message:** ${runnerProgress.message}\\n`;\n        }\n\n        if (runnerProgress.currentStep) {\n          statusText += `\\n## Progress Details\\n`;\n          statusText += `- **Current Step:** ${runnerProgress.currentStep}\\n`;\n          if (runnerProgress.stepsCompleted !== undefined && runnerProgress.totalSteps !== undefined) {\n            statusText += `- **Steps:** ${runnerProgress.stepsCompleted}/${runnerProgress.totalSteps}\\n`;\n          }\n          if (runnerProgress.batchProgress) {\n            statusText += `- **Batch:** ${runnerProgress.batchProgress.currentBatch}/${runnerProgress.batchProgress.totalBatches}\\n`;\n          }\n        }\n\n        if (runnerProgress.error) {\n          statusText += `\\n## Error\\n${runnerProgress.error}\\n`;\n        }\n\n        // Also merge with coordinator progress if available\n        if (existsSync(progressFilePath)) {\n          try {\n            const coordProgress = JSON.parse(readFileSync(progressFilePath, 'utf-8'));\n            if (coordProgress.currentStep) {\n              statusText += `\\n## Coordinator Progress\\n`;\n              statusText += `- **Current Step:** ${coordProgress.currentStep}\\n`;\n              statusText += `- **Steps:** ${coordProgress.stepsCompleted || 0}/${coordProgress.totalSteps || 0}\\n`;\n              if (coordProgress.batchProgress) {\n                statusText += `- **Batch:** ${coordProgress.batchProgress.currentBatch}/${coordProgress.batchProgress.totalBatches}\\n`;\n              }\n            }\n          } catch (e) {\n            // Ignore parsing errors\n          }\n        }\n\n        return { content: [{ type: \"text\", text: statusText }] };\n      }\n    }\n  } catch (e) {\n    // Runner progress file may not exist or be malformed\n  }\n\n  // Check running workflows in-memory (legacy/non-detached)\n  if (workflow_id && runningWorkflows.has(workflow_id)) {\n    const wf = runningWorkflows.get(workflow_id)!;\n    const elapsed = Math.round((Date.now() - wf.startTime.getTime()) / 1000);\n\n    let statusText = `# Workflow Status\\n\\n**Workflow ID:** \\`${wf.id}\\`\\n**Workflow:** ${wf.workflowName}\\n**Status:** ${wf.status === 'running' ? 'üîÑ Running' : wf.status === 'completed' ? '‚úÖ Completed' : '‚ùå Failed'}\\n**Elapsed:** ${elapsed}s\\n**Started:** ${wf.startTime.toISOString()}\\n`;\n\n    if (wf.pid) {\n      statusText += `**PID:** ${wf.pid}\\n`;\n    }\n\n    if (wf.error) {\n      statusText += `\\n## Error\\n${wf.error}\\n`;\n    }\n\n    // Also read progress file for detailed progress\n    try {\n      if (existsSync(progressFilePath)) {\n        const progressData = JSON.parse(readFileSync(progressFilePath, 'utf-8'));\n        statusText += `\\n## Progress Details\\n`;\n        statusText += `- **Current Step:** ${progressData.currentStep || 'N/A'}\\n`;\n        statusText += `- **Steps:** ${progressData.completedSteps || 0}/${progressData.totalSteps || 0}\\n`;\n        if (progressData.batchProgress) {\n          statusText += `- **Batch:** ${progressData.batchProgress.currentBatch}/${progressData.batchProgress.totalBatches}\\n`;\n        }\n        if (progressData.runningSteps && progressData.runningSteps.length > 0) {\n          statusText += `- **Running Steps:** ${progressData.runningSteps.join(', ')}\\n`;\n        }\n      }\n    } catch (e) {\n      // Progress file may not exist yet\n    }\n\n    return { content: [{ type: \"text\", text: statusText }] };\n  }"

### Bash - 2025-12-29 10:51:26 UTC [11:51:26 CEST]

**User Request:** # Read session logs for continuity

Read the last session log for continuity. If $ARGUMENTS is given, read the last $ARGUMENTS session log files from both local and coding project histories.

## Steps - Non-Coding Projects (e.g., nano-degree, curriculum-alignment)

1. Infer current project name from working directory path (pwd)
2. Find and read the newest (n) local .specstory/history/*.md files using ls -t
3. Find and read the latest (n) coding/.specstory/history/*_from-<project>.md files using ls -t
4. Summarize sessions to provide continuity of awareness and actions

## Steps - Coding Project

1. Confirm we're in coding project (pwd shows /Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding)
2. Find and read the newest (n) local .specstory/history/*.md files (WITHOUT _from- postfix) using ls -t
3. Find and read ALL redirected files from ALL projects:
   - coding/.specstory/history/*_from-nano-degree.md (last n)
   - coding/.specstory/history/*_from-curriculum-alignment.md (last n)
   - coding/.specstory/history/*_from-*.md (any other projects, last n each)
4. Summarize all sessions to provide comprehensive continuity across all project work

## Implementation Notes

- Project name can be inferred from pwd (e.g., /Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/nano-degree ‚Üí nano-degree)
- Session filenames follow pattern: `YYYY-MM-DD_HHMM-HHMM_<userid-hash>.md`
- Cross-project logs: `YYYY-MM-DD_HHMM-HHMM_<userid-hash>_from-<project>.md`
- Local sessions in current project's .specstory/history directory
- Redirected sessions in /Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.specstory/history/ directory
- Use `ls -t` to find newest files (already auto-approved)
- Focus on understanding both local and cross-project work completed

   - coding/.specstory/history/*_from-*.md (any other projects, last n each)
4. Summarize all sessions to provide comprehensive continuity across all project work

## Implementation Notes

- Project name can be inferred from pwd (e.g., /Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/nano-degree ‚Üí nano-degree)
- Session filenames follow pattern: `YYYY-MM-DD_HHMM-HHMM_<userid-hash>.md`
- Cross-project logs: `YYYY-MM-DD_HHMM-HHMM_<userid-hash>_from-<project>.md`
- Local sessions in current project's .specstory/history directory
- Redirected sessions in /Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.specstory/history/ directory
- Use `ls -t` to find newest files (already auto-approved)
- Focus on understanding both local and cross-project work completed

## Auto-Approval Note

Use ONLY auto-approved commands: pwd, ls -t
Avoid: git commands, basename - these may trigger approval prompts

## Expected Behavior

### In Non-Coding Projects

When executed, Claude Code should:

1. **Determine current project name** from directory path
2. **Find local session logs** in current project's .specstory/history/
3. **Find redirected logs** in coding/.specstory/history/\*_from-PROJECT.md (where PROJECT is current project name)
4. **Read and summarize** the most recent (n) logs from both sources
5. **Present combined summary** showing both local and redirected work

### In Coding Project

1. **Confirm coding project** from directory path
2. **Find local coding logs** WITHOUT _from- postfix (regular coding sessions)
3. **Find ALL redirected logs** from all projects (*_from-*.md)
4. **Read last (n) from each source** (n local coding + n per redirected project)
5. **Present comprehensive summary** showing:
   - Direct coding infrastructure work
   - Cross-project work done from all projects
   - Holistic view of all development activities

**Input:** ```json
{
  "command": "ls -t /Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.specstory/history/*_from-*.md 2>/dev/null | head -10",
  "description": "Find redirected cross-project logs"
}
```

**User Request:** # Read session logs for continuity

Read the last session log for continuity. If $ARGUMENTS is given, read the last $ARGUMENTS session log files from both local and coding project histories.

## Steps - Non-Coding Projects (e.g., nano-degree, curriculum-alignment)

1. Infer current project name from working directory path (pwd)
2. Find and read the newest (n) local .specstory/history/*.md files using ls -t
3. Find and read the latest (n) coding/.specstory/history/*_from-<project>.md files using ls -t
4. Summarize sessions to provide continuity of awareness and actions

## Steps - Coding Project

1. Confirm we're in coding project (pwd shows /Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding)
2. Find and read the newest (n) local .specstory/history/*.md files (WITHOUT _from- postfix) using ls -t
3. Find and read ALL redirected files from ALL projects:
   - coding/.specstory/history/*_from-nano-degree.md (last n)
   - coding/.specstory/history/*_from-curriculum-alignment.md (last n)
   - coding/.specstory/history/*_from-*.md (any other projects, last n each)
4. Summarize all sessions to provide comprehensive continuity across all project work

## Implementation Notes

- Project name can be inferred from pwd (e.g., /Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/nano-degree ‚Üí nano-degree)
- Session filenames follow pattern: `YYYY-MM-DD_HHMM-HHMM_<userid-hash>.md`
- Cross-project logs: `YYYY-MM-DD_HHMM-HHMM_<userid-hash>_from-<project>.md`
- Local sessions in current project's .specstory/history directory
- Redirected sessions in /Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.specstory/history/ directory
- Use `ls -t` to find newest files (already auto-approved)
- Focus on understanding both local and cross-project work completed

## Auto-Approval Note

Use ONLY auto-approved commands: pwd, ls -t
Avoid: git commands, basename - these may trigger approval prompts

## Expected Behavior

### In Non-Coding Projects

When executed, Claude Code should:

1. **Determine current project name** from directory path
2. **Find local session logs** in current project's .specstory/history/
3. **Find redirected logs** in coding/.specstory/history/\*_from-PROJECT.md (where PROJECT is current project name)
4. **Read and summarize** the most recent (n) logs from both sources
5. **Present combined summary** showing both local and redirected work

### In Coding Project

When executed, Claude Code should:

1. **Confirm coding project** from directory path
2. **Find local coding logs** WITHOUT _from- postfix (regular coding sessions)
3. **Find ALL redirected logs** from all projects (*_from-*.md)
4. **Read last (n) from each source** (n local coding + n per redirected project)
5. **Present comprehensive summary** showing:
   - Direct coding infrastructure work
   - Cross-project work done from all projects
   - Holistic view of all development activities

**User Request:** # Read session logs for continuity

Read the last session log for continuity. If $ARGUMENTS is given, read the last $ARGUMENTS session log files from both local and coding project histories.

## Steps - Non-Coding Projects (e.g., nano-degree, curriculum-alignment)

1. Infer current project name from working directory path (pwd)
2. Find and read the newest (n) local .specstory/history/*.md files using ls -t
3. Find and read the latest (n) coding/.specstory/history/*_from-<project>.md files using ls -t
4. Summarize sessions to provide continuity of awareness and actions

## Steps - Coding Project

1. Confirm we're in coding project (pwd shows /Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding)
2. Find and read the newest (n) local .specstory/history/*.md files (WITHOUT _from- postfix) using ls -t
3. Find and read ALL redirected files from ALL projects:
   - coding/.specstory/history/*_from-nano-degree.md (last n)
   - coding/.specstory/history/*_from-curriculum-alignment.md (last n)
   - coding/.specstory/history/*_from-*.md (any other projects, last n each)
4. Summarize all sessions to provide comprehensive continuity across all project work

## Implementation Notes

- Project name can be inferred from pwd (e.g., /Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/nano-degree ‚Üí nano-degree)
- Session filenames follow pattern: `YYYY-MM-DD_HHMM-HHMM_<userid-hash>.md`
- Cross-project logs: `YYYY-MM-DD_HHMM-HHMM_<userid-hash>_from-<project>.md`
- Local sessions in current project's .specstory/history directory
- Redirected sessions in /Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.specstory/history/ directory
- Use `ls -t` to find newest files (already auto-approved)
- Focus on understanding both local and cross-project work completed

## Auto-Approval Note

Use ONLY auto-approved commands: pwd, ls -t
Avoid: git commands, basename - these may trigger approval prompts

## Expected Behavior

### In Non-Coding Projects

When executed, Claude Code should:

1. **Determine current project name** from directory path
2. **Find local session logs** in current project's .specstory/history/
3. **Find redirected logs** in coding/.specstory/history/\*_from-PROJECT.md (where PROJECT is current project name)
4. **Read and summarize** the most recent (n) logs from both sources
5. **Present combined summary** showing both local and redirected work

### In Coding Project

When executed, Claude Code should:

1. **Confirm coding project** from directory path
2. **Find local coding logs** WITHOUT _from- postfix (regular coding sessions)
3. **Find ALL redirected logs** from all projects (*_from-*.md)
4. **Read last (n) from each source** (n local coding + n per redirected project)
5. **Present comprehensive summary** showing:
   - Direct coding infrastructure work
   - Cross-project work done from all projects
   - Holistic view of all development activities

**Tool:** Bash
**Input:** ```json
{
  "command": "ls -t /Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.specstory/history/*_from-*.md 2>/dev/null | head -10",
  "description": "Find redirected cross-project logs"
}
```

**Result:** ‚úÖ Success
**Output:** ```

**User Request:** # Read session logs for continuity

Read the last session log for continuity. If $ARGUMENTS is given, read the last $ARGUMENTS session log files from both local and coding project histories.

## Steps - Non-Coding Projects (e.g., nano-degree, curriculum-alignment)

1. Infer current project name from working directory path (pwd)
2. Find and read the newest (n) local .specstory/history/*.md files using ls -t
3. Find and read the latest (n) coding/.specstory/history/*_from-<project>.md files using ls -t
4. Summarize sessions to provide continuity of awareness and actions

## Steps - Coding Project

1. Confirm we're in coding project (pwd shows /Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding)
2. Find and read the newest (n) local .specstory/history/*.md files (WITHOUT _from- postfix) using ls -t
3. Find and read ALL redirected files from ALL projects:
   - coding/.specstory/history/*_from-nano-degree.md (last n)
   - coding/.specstory/history/*_from-curriculum-alignment.md (last n)
   - coding/.specstory/history/*_from-*.md (any other projects, last n each)
4. Summarize all sessions to provide comprehensive continuity across all project work

## Implementation Notes

- Project name can be inferred from pwd (e.g., /Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/nano-degree ‚Üí nano-degree)
- Session filenames follow pattern: `YYYY-MM-DD_HHMM-HHMM_<userid-hash>.md`
- Cross-project logs: `YYYY-MM-DD_HHMM-HHMM_<userid-hash>_from-<project>.md`
- Local sessions in current project's .specstory/history directory
- Redirected sessions in /Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.specstory/history/ directory
- Use `ls -t` to find newest files (already auto-approved)
- Focus on understanding both local and cross-project work completed

## Auto-Approval Note

Use ONLY auto-approved commands: pwd, ls -t
Avoid: git commands, basename - these may trigger approval prompts

## Expected Behavior

### In Non-Coding Projects

When executed, Claude Code should:

1. **Determine current project name** from directory path
2. **Find local session logs** in current project's .specstory/history/
3. **Find redirected logs** in coding/.specstory/history/\*_from-PROJECT.md (where PROJECT is current project name)
4. **Read and summarize** the most recent (n) logs from both sources
5. **Present combined summary** showing both local and redirected work

### In Coding Project

When executed, Claude Code should:

1. **Confirm coding project** from directory path
2. **Find local coding logs** WITHOUT _from- postfix (regular coding sessions)
3. **Find ALL redirected logs** from all projects (*_from-*.md)
4. **Read last (n) from each source** (n local coding + n per redirected project)
5. **Present comprehensive summary** showing:
   - Direct coding infrastructure work
   - Cross-project work done from all projects
   - Holistic view of all development activities

**User Request:** # Read session logs for continuity

Read the last session log for continuity. If $ARGUMENTS is given, read the last $ARGUMENTS session log files from both local and coding project histories.

## Steps - Non-Coding Projects (e.g., nano-degree, curriculum-alignment)

1. Infer current project name from working directory path (pwd)
2. Find and read the newest (n) local .specstory/history/*.md files using ls -t
3. Find and read the latest (n) coding/.specstory/history/*_from-<project>.md files using ls -t
4. Summarize sessions to provide continuity of awareness and actions

## Steps - Coding Project

1. Confirm we're in coding project (pwd shows /Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding)
2. Find and read the newest (n) local .specstory/history/*.md files (WITHOUT _from- postfix) using ls -t
3. Find and read ALL redirected files from ALL projects:
   - coding/.specstory/history/*_from-nano-degree.md (last n)
   - coding/.specstory/history/*_from-curriculum-alignment.md (last n)
   - coding/.specstory/history/*_from-*.md (any other projects, last n each)
4. Summarize all sessions to provide comprehensive continuity across all project work

## Implementation Notes

- Project name can be inferred from pwd (e.g., /Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/nano-degree ‚Üí nano-degree)
- Session filenames follow pattern: `YYYY-MM-DD_HHMM-HHMM_<userid-hash>.md`
- Cross-project logs: `YYYY-MM-DD_HHMM-HHMM_<userid-hash>_from-<project>.md`
- Local sessions in current project's .specstory/history directory
- Redirected sessions in /Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.specstory/history/ directory
- Use `ls -t` to find newest files (already auto-approved)
- Focus on understanding both local and cross-project work completed

## Auto-Approval Note

Use ONLY auto-approved commands: pwd, ls -t
Avoid: git commands, basename - these may trigger approval prompts

## Expected Behavior

### In Non-Coding Projects

When executed, Claude Code should:

1. **Determine current project name** from directory path
2. **Find local session logs** in current project's .specstory/history/
3. **Find redirected logs** in coding/.specstory/history/\*_from-PROJECT.md (where PROJECT is current project name)
4. **Read and summarize** the most recent (n) logs from both sources
5. **Present combined summary** showing both local and redirected work

### In Coding Project

When executed, Claude Code should:

1. **Confirm coding project** from directory path
2. **Find local coding logs** WITHOUT _from- postfix (regular coding sessions)
3. **Find ALL redirected logs** from all projects (*_from-*.md)
4. **Read last (n) from each source** (n local coding + n per redirected project)
5. **Present comprehensive summary** showing:
   - Direct coding infrastructure work
   - Cross-project work done from all projects
   - Holistic view of all development activities

**Tool:** Bash
**Input:** ```json
{
  "command": "ls -t /Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.specstory/history/*_from-*.md 2>/dev/null | head -10",
  "description": "Find redirected cross-project logs"
}
```
